createTestU2FDevice(t *testing.T, name string, counter uint32) *types.MFADevice {\n\t// Generate a test ECDSA key pair\n\tprivateKey, err := ecdsa.GenerateKey(elliptic.P256(), rand.Reader)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to generate key: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create a unique, deterministic key handle based on the counter and name\n\t// This ensures each device has a different key handle\n\thashInput := fmt.Sprintf(\"u2f-device-%s-%d-%d\", name, counter, time.Now().UnixNano())\n\th := sha256.Sum256([]byte(hashInput))\n\tkeyHandle := h[:]\n\n\t// Create device\n\tdevice := types.NewMFADevice(name, time.Now())\n\tdevice.Id = fmt.Sprintf(\"device-id-%d\", counter)\n\n\t// Marshal the public key to DER format using x509\n\tpubKeyDER, err := x509.MarshalPKIXPublicKey(&privateKey.PublicKey)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to marshal public key: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tdevice.Device = &types.MFADevice_U2F{\n\t\tU2F:
